# Dungeons

Dungeons are PvE raid activities in which a team of 1 to 5 players work together to defeat mobs within a procedurally generated series of rooms , ending in a boss fight. Players are rewarded based on their performance within the Dungeon with Dungeoneering XP and items within chests . The rewards scale up with the difficulty of the Dungeon; the more difficult missions can drop some of the strongest items in the game.
Currently, the only released Dungeons are the Catacombs and its Master Mode . Two other Dungeons have been hinted at with a desert and forest theme.
Normally, you must have a party of at least 2 players to start a dungeon run, with the exception of Ⓑ Bingo profiles. However, if you have completed Floor III and defeated The Professor , you may claim Saul's Recommendation and give it to Mort , who will then let you run dungeons alone.
If a player has the requirements to enter a floor solo, sometimes they will go into the floor and get to the blood room as fast as they can, and will kill The Watcher 's resurrected giants for their fragments. This is how the money-making method "Frag Running" is done on Floor VII .
Completing a new dungeon floor (including Master Mode) rewards SkyBlock XP, which is used to level up an important stat called SkyBlock Levels .

## Mechanics

### Overview
Dungeons consist of a series of connected rooms. The main goal of each Dungeon run is to unlock each door, beat The Watcher guarding the way to the boss room, then defeat the boss. Along the way, special Dungeon Mobs will spawn and attack the player. Certain Dungeon rooms will also contain special items and buffs to help players accomplish their goal.

### Generation
Each Dungeon is a series of rooms connected by doorways. The path to the Blood Room is always guarded by a series of Wither doors, and the Blood Door at the end; the Fairy room will always generate along this path.
The size and number of rooms in each Dungeon depends on the listed size:
  Dungeon Size
  Size in rooms
  Tiny
  4x4
  Small
  5x5
  Medium
  5x6 6x6
Within each Dungeon, the following special rooms will always generate:
- Starting room - Green Room
- At least 2 puzzle rooms - Purple Room
- Mini-boss room - Yellow Room
- Fairy room - Pink Room
- Blood room - Red Room
- Trap room (Floor III + only) - Orange Room
The rest of the space is filled in with normal rooms - Brown Rooms.
Special rooms are always generated in 1x1 space, and generate at the end of a chain of connected rooms. Normal rooms can generate in a 1x1 , 1x2 , 1x3 , 1x4 , 2x2 or L-shaped space.
Dungeon Mobs spawn in all normal rooms. Their spawning locations are set, and in some cases their type, as in Lonely Spider spawns in the spider room.
Each room also has a number of Dungeon Secrets , which appear in fixed locations. Each Secret, when found, awards the player with loot or a team-wide buff called Blessings, and adds to the score for that run.
A Magical Map of the Dungeon replaces the SkyBlock Menu once the Dungeon begins. This map shows the location of all rooms as well as their completion status. It is taken away once entering the boss room. When right-clicked, it functions as a SkyBlock Menu.

### Gear Mechanics
Most items obtained from Dungeons with stats are Dungeon items; normal items can be converted to Dungeon items with Essence . Dungeon items can be differentiated from normal items in the rarity, for example, " RARE DUNGEON SWORD ".
Dungeon items receive stat buffs according to the Dungeon level of its user. In addition, certain items can be upgraded with Essence, which applies up to five stars to the item. Each star adds a 2-10% buff outside of Dungeons and 10%-50% inside the Dungeon. The Dungeon level and star stat buffs are additive; if a player has a 20% stat buff from levels and 50% from stars, the total stat buff will be 70%. If a slayer item is converted into a Dungeon item with Essence, it can be used within Dungeons even if the player does not have Slayer level requirement of that item. Please note that all stats are boosted by the General's Medallion .
The following stats are boosted by both Dungeon levels and stars:
- ❤ Health (e.g. Sniper Helmet )
- ❈ Defense (e.g. Bonzo's Mask )
- ❁ Strength (e.g. Flower of Truth )
- ❁ Damage (e.g. Giant's Sword )
- ✦ Speed (e.g. Shadow Fury )
- ☠ Crit Damage (e.g. Livid Dagger )
- ✎ Intelligence (e.g. Precursor Eye )
- α Sea Creature Chance (e.g. Chimera Weapon with Ammonite Pet )
- ✧ Pristine (e.g. Previous Maxor's Armor with Topaz Gemstone equipped)
- ⸕ Mining Speed (e.g. Chimera Weapon with Scatha Pet )
- ☘ Mining Fortune (e.g. Chimera Weapon with a Pet that has a Quick Claw )
- ☘ Farming Fortune (e.g. Chimera Weapon with Mooshroom Cow Pet )
The following stats are only boosted by stars:
- ✯ Magic Find (e.g. Divine Gift Weapon)
- ❂ True Defense (e.g. Astraea )
- ☣ Crit Chance (e.g. Livid Dagger )
- ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed (e.g. Zombie Soldier Cutlass )
- ⫽ Ferocity (e.g. Valkyrie )
- ๑ Ability Damage (e.g. Wither Goggles )
For the following stats, it is unknown how they are boosted:
- ♣ Pet Luck (e.g. Chimera Weapon with Endermite Pet )
- ☘ Foraging Fortune
Most Dungeon items, including converted items, require a certain Dungeon level to use. In addition, gear dropped from mobs from a Floor have the same Dungeon level requirement as the requirement to enter that Floor, but only in that Dungeon. For example, a Zombie Knight Armor piece dropped from Floor VII will require Catacombs 14 to use, as well as Catacombs 24 within the Catacombs.

### General Mechanics
Certain mechanics are tweaked within Dungeons:
- Every time you hit an enemy, you regain 1% max +5 ✎ Mana . This applies to: Melee strikes Bow hits Mage Staff ability (for Mage class)
- Melee strikes
- Bow hits
- Mage Staff ability (for Mage class)
- This does not apply to: Item abilities ( Spirit Sceptre ability, etc.) Class abilities (Explosive Shot, etc.)
- Item abilities ( Spirit Sceptre ability, etc.)
- Class abilities (Explosive Shot, etc.)
- The Purse is not displayed. The bonus from items buffed by the Purse ( Emerald Blade , etc.) will not work. Shops in the Dungeon will first take from the purse, then directly from the player's bank.
- Any ✦ Speed above 100 is reduced by 1/3 .
- The following enchantments are changed: Dragon Tracer is disabled. Healing from Vampirism is reduced 10x . Slowing effect from Venomous is reduced.
- Dragon Tracer is disabled.
- Healing from Vampirism is reduced 10x .
- Slowing effect from Venomous is reduced.
- The following items are changed: The item ability of the End Stone Sword does not work. All fired arrows do not respect invincibility frames, but deal reduced knockback.
- The item ability of the End Stone Sword does not work.
- All fired arrows do not respect invincibility frames, but deal reduced knockback.
- The player is not allowed to do the following: Warp to private islands (warping to the Hub and other locations is still allowed). Ride mounts such as the Horse Pet . Use /ah, /et, /av or /bz with the Cookie Buff on.
- Warp to private islands (warping to the Hub and other locations is still allowed).
- Ride mounts such as the Horse Pet .
- Use /ah, /et, /av or /bz with the Cookie Buff on.
- Players may only consume or splash one potion during a Dungeon run. Healing, Mana and Stamina potions are exceptions. Players can receive effects from multiple potions if they are splashed or consumed simultaneously. God Potions may not be consumed.
- Healing, Mana and Stamina potions are exceptions.
- Players can receive effects from multiple potions if they are splashed or consumed simultaneously.
- God Potions may not be consumed.

### Floors
Each Dungeon contains a number of Floors. Each Floor is harder than the previous by about 50%, but better loot.
  Catacombs
  7 + 1 entrance
  Master Mode
In order to enter a Floor, the player must have completed the Floor before it at least once and has to have the required Dungeon level.

Certain Dungeon items require the player to have completed a floor before it can be used. For example, Shadow Assassin Armor requires a Floor V completion.

### Classes
Currently, there are five playable classes within Dungeons:
- Healer - Uses their healing abilities and tools to keep the team alive and dealing ❁ Damage .
- Berserk - Specialises in close-quarter combat, relying on Life Steal and high melee ❁ Damage to defeat enemies.
- Mage - Relies on high ✎ Intelligence levels and magic ❁ Damage to shut enemies down with magic weapons. Its Mage Staff ability deals formidable single-target ❁ Damage from a safe distance.
- Archer - Ranged weapons allow it to take down high-health enemies from a safe distance.
- Tank - Keeps the team safe by drawing enemy attention away from and taking ❁ Damage on behalf of more vulnerable members of the team.
Each class gains class-specific buffs and abilities within Dungeons. The power of those buffs and abilities are increased by leveling up those classes. Class abilities can be used with the Dungeon Orb , or by pressing the drop (ultimate) or drop stack (regular) key with an Orb in inventory.
If within a Dungeon run there is only one instance of a class, the class buffs are increased by 100% of their base stats. For example, if a level 25 Archer (50% base extra arrow chance, 25% additional extra arrow chance from levels) is the only Archer in a run, their extra arrow chance will be increased to 125%.
- Healer
- Mage
- Berserk
- Archer
- Tank
Class Passives Renew : Your healing abilities heal the target for 50% additional ❤ HP . Grants 1.5x ☄ Mending , which increases your healing on others. Healing Aura : Passively heals all living teammates within a 8 block radius for 1% ❤ HP per second. Revive : Spawns a fairy that follows you and uses it's energy to revives dead teammates, while no-one is dead it will stick around and provide support. Vanishes for 100 seconds after reviving a player. Orbies : Enemies that you help kill have a 15% chance to drop an orb that anyone can pick up. The orb heals the player that picked it up and grants them a random buff. Soul Tether : Clicking on a teammate creates a tether connecting yourself to them. Tethered teammates received 0.5% of your maximum ❤ Health as healing every second while they are within 30 blocks of you. Every 5 melee hits you deal while tethered will heal both players for 1% of their maximum ❤ Health . Overheal : Healing a player that is full health will convert the healing into an absorption shield up to 20% of their ❤ Health .
Dungeon Stone Abilities Healing Circle : Launches a healing orb that creates a healing circle where it lands. The healing circle heals friendly players inside for 2% of their ❤ Health every second. Cooldown: 2 seconds Wish : Heals everyone in your group to full health and grants them a shields for 20% of their maximum health. The cooldown is reduced by 10 seconds for every player below 25% health. Cooldown: 120 seconds
Ghost Abilities Healing Potion : Throw a potion which heals all teammates in a 10 block radius for 10% of their max health and +100 ❤ Health Revive : Revive yourself after 50 seconds.
Leveling Bonus You can level up the Healer class while playing as a Healer or if you have a teammate that is Healer, you get some of its Healer XP as a team bonus.
For every healer level you get:
- +1% Renew Healing
- +2 Ghost Healing Potion Health Restored

- -1 Revive Cooldown
- +0.4% Overheal Maximum Shield
For every other healer level you also get:
- +1% Ghost Healing aura Healing

- +0.1% Healing aura Healing
- +0.5% Healing Circle Healing
- +0.5 Healing Circle Radius
- +1 Healing Circle Duration
- +250 ✎ Intelligence
Class Passives Mage Staff : All your melee weapon attacks become ranged. Those attacks deal 30% of their melee ❁ Damage (increased by your ✎ Intelligence ) up to 10 blocks, after which damage is reduced. Formula for Mage Staff damage is: M e l e e D a m a g e × ( 0.3 + 0.0009 × I n t e l l i g e n c e ) {\textstyle {MeleeDamage \times (0.3 + 0.0009 \times Intelligence)}} Efficient Spells : All abilities have a 25% shorter cooldown.

Ruduces the cooldown remaining on Throwing Axe by 1 second on activation. Heals you for 3% of your ❤ Health every melee hit. The Guided Sheep , Explosive Shot and Seismic Wave abilities can blow up crypts and walls like Superboom TNT does.

### Loot
Dungeon loot is obtained in three ways: from Secrets , dropped from mobs or bought from Dungeon Reward Chests .

### Death and Revival
In Dungeons, instead of dying, players become Ghosts, where they are invisible except for a ghost icon that follows them and is visible to other players. Players also become Ghosts if they leave and return to the dungeon for any reason. In the Ghost state, players can fly freely, but not through walls. They are unable to normally interact with the world, except for killing Fairies in order to revive themselves, and through the use of their respective Ghost Abilities.
In Ghost form, players are unable to use the majority of the features in the SkyBlock Menu, or warp out of the Dungeon. Ghosts cannot attack Dungeon Mobs , with the exception of through their Ghost Abilities. For additional ghost abilities, players can get the Spirit Sword and Spirit Shortbow , both of which appear in the player's hotbar when the player is dead, if they had the items beforehand. These are usable as normal. They also gain the Haunt ability, which teleports them to a chosen alive teammate. Ghosts are also able to view the Magical Map .
Ghosts may be revived in the following ways:
- Having a Revive Stone in their inventory prior to death.
- Having a teammate use a Revive Stone.
- Killing a Fairy in a Fairy Room.
- Defeating the corresponding Wandering Soul in The Watcher boss fight.
- By the Revive passive and Revive ghost ability of the Healer class.
- Automatically after 15 seconds on Entrance, 45 seconds on Floor I , and 100 seconds on Floor II .
- Entering a boss fight (all teammates in the dungeon are revived beforehand)

### Finishing, Scoring and Rewards
The Dungeon is finished when one of the following occurs:
- The Boss is defeated.
- All players in the Dungeon have either died and become Ghosts or left the dungeon.
- 60 minutes pass without defeating the Boss. In practice, a few more minutes may be allowed before the run is forcibly failed.
- In practice, a few more minutes may be allowed before the run is forcibly failed.
Players need not complete every room or kill every mob to complete the dungeon.
At the end of the Dungeon, a Score is assigned to the run depending on how much of the Dungeon has been explored, the number of Secrets found, the number of times the players died, the number of puzzles failed and the time taken to clear the Dungeon. If the Dungeon boss is completed, the player is offered up to six Dungeon Reward Chests , which contain rewards of loot and Essence and can be opened for a cost.

## Trivia
- The Dungeoneering skill is most likely a reference to the skill of the same name in RuneScape , where it is mainly leveled up in Daemonheim, where players complete randomly generated dungeons. Likewise, Dungeons uses similar mechanics.

# Catacombs

The Catacombs is the first Dungeon in SkyBlock. It can be accessed through speaking to Mort in the ⏣ Catacombs Entrance or ⏣ Dungeon Hub .
Players are, by default, required to be in a party of 2 - 5 players in order to join the Catacombs: giving Mort a Saul's Recommendation from Adventurer Saul allows players to enter the Catacombs on their own. You can set up your own party and invite your friends to join, or you can set up a party through the Party Finder , where you can select different options and requirements for people to join your party.

## Overview
The Catacombs are a series of floors, each with interconnecting rooms filled with mobs , secrets , and other obstacles. After killing enough mobs, you are guaranteed to drop a Wither Key , which unlocks more sections of the floor: the Blood Key will unlock the Blood Room , where The Watcher summons Undead that must be killed in order to progress to the boss room.
While in the Catacombs , several restrictions are imposed:
- All purchases from Dungeon Reward Chests or NPCs take coins directly from your Bank . Players will not have a purse.
- All ✦ Speed above 100 ✦ Speed is reduced by 33.3% .
- Players may not warp to their Private Island .
- Players may not Auction House , Bazaar , and Anvil , even while under the effect of a Booster Cookie .
- Players may not summon mounts, like the Horse , Skeleton Horse , Armadillo , or Pig Pet .
- Only one potion may be consumed per run, with the exception of Stamina , Healing , and Mana Potions . God Potions cannot be consumed.
- Arrows deal reduced knockback.
- ❁ Damage against bosses is reduced above certain thresholds, depending on the boss.
- Dragon Tracer is explicitly disabled, healing from Vampirism is reduced by 10x , and slowness from Venomous is greatly reduced.

### Classes
Players can choose one of five Classes : Berserk , Archer , Mage , Tank , and Healer . Each class serves a different purpose and has their own abilities, class passives, and ghost abilities. They are more effective if only one of each are present in a party, although multiple players can choose the same class if they wish.
- Berserks prioritize dealing as much melee ❁ Damage as possible.
- Archers prioritize dealing as much ranged ❁ Damage as possible.
- Mages prioritize using their item abilities to deal as much magic damage as possible. A sub-sect of Mage, known as Left-Click Mage , uses their Mage Staff passive to deal high amounts of melee ❁ Damage .
- A sub-sect of Mage, known as Left-Click Mage , uses their Mage Staff passive to deal high amounts of melee ❁ Damage .
- Tanks prioritize staying near their teammates and receiving as much ❁ Damage as possible.
- Healers prioritize providing healing and support to their teammates and themselves.

### Ghosts
When a player loses all their ❤ Health in the Catacombs , they do not die traditionally: instead, they turn into a Ghost and function as a spectator with unique abilities and limited access to the SkyBlock Menu .
Ghosts can only interact with the environment through their abilities: these abilities depend on their chosen Class , and are listed below.
  Class
  Name
  Ability
  Berserk
  Buff Potion
  Throws a potion that temporarily gives all teammates in a 10 block radius +30 ❁ Strength . Has a 20s cooldown.
  Ghost Axe
  Throws an axe that deals damage based on your Berserk level. Has a 10s cooldown.
  Archer
  Stun Bow
  Temporarily stuns its target upon hit: does not affect bosses. Has a 10s cooldown.
  Healing Bow
  Can be used to shoot a teammate, healing them for 20% of their max ❤ Health and granting them +50 ❁ Strength for 10s . Has a 10s cooldown.
  Mage
  Instant Wall
  Spawns a 5 x 3 wall on the block you are looking at for 10s . Has a 20s cooldown.
  Fireball
  Throws an fireball that deals damage based on your Mage level. Has a 10s cooldown.
  Tank
  Stun Potion
  Throws a potion that temporarily stuns all monsters in a 10 block radius. Has a 20s cooldown.
  Absorption Potion
  Throws a potion that gives all teammates in a +200 ❤ Absorption for 3s , multiplied by your Tank level * 10 . Has a 20s cooldown.
  Healer
  Revive
  Revive yourself after 50s .
  Healing Potion
  Throws a potion that heals all teammates in a 10 block radius for 10% of their max ❤ Health and +100 ❤ Health , multiplied by 100 + your Healer level * 2 . Has a 20s cooldown.

## Floors
The Catacombs has 7 floors and 1 entrance: beating a floor unlocks the one succeeding it. Defeating Necron , the boss of The Catacombs - Floor VII , unlocks Master Mode , a harder version of the Catacombs will be available.

## Rooms and Exploration
The Magical Map replaces the SkyBlock Menu while in the main section of a Catacombs floor: it provides a map that shows the layout of the dungeon as it is explored and completed. There are several different rooms in the Catacombs, organized by colour:
  Room
  Description
  Starter Room
  The Starter Room is the room where the Dungeon begins: players can ready up and change their class in this room before the run starts. Mort can be found here, and he gives players a Dungeon Orb on lower floors.
  Standard Room
  Each Dungeon run mostly consists of Standard Rooms . They contain a multitude of mobs and secrets: some mobs will have a yellow star next to their names, marking them as unique. When all unique mobs, or a miniboss, are killed, they will drop an item and mark the room as complete: two of these are guaranteed to be a Wither Key , and one of these is guaranteed to be a Blood Key .
  Puzzle Room
  The Puzzle Room contains a Puzzle that must be completed for the room to be marked as completed. Some can be failed, and others cannot: they can be reset with an Architect's First Draft .
  Miniboss Room
  The Miniboss Room contains a random 5 Mini-Boss : killing them will mark the room as complete. The miniboss can be a Angry Archaeologist , Lost Adventurer , King Midas , Shadow Assassin , or Frozen Adventurer .
  Trap Room
  The Trap Room consists of several traps and obstacles that must be overcome. They contain several secrets that must be all completed in order to mark the room as complete.
  Fairy Room
  The Fairy Room consists of a large tree in the middle, with several Fairies surrounding it that drop a Revive Stone when killed. A healing pool can be found near the tree.
  Blood Room
  The Blood Room is the final room that must be completed before the boss room can be accessed. The Watcher will summon lots of Undead that must be all killed in order for the room to be marked as completed: on higher floors, they will receive modifiers and some will take the appearance of previous bosses, like Bonzo , Scarf , the Spirit Bear , or Sadan's Giants .

## Exploration and Rewards

### Dungeon Score
Dungeon Score is a value comprised of four categories: Skill , or the number of deaths and puzzles failed in a run; Exploration , or the percentage of the floor completed and the number of secrets completed; Speed , or the time taken to complete a run; and Bonus , which varies depending on the floor and active modifiers, like Paul 's EZPZ perk.
- 0-99 Score grants a D .
- 100-159 Score grants a C .
- 160-229 Score grants a B .
- 230-269.4 Score grants a A .
- 270-300 Score grants a S .
- ≥300 Score grants a S+ .
For more in-depth calculations, see Dungeon Score .

### Dungeon Reward Chests
When a party or player successfully completes a Dungeon run, they can spend coins to unlock different tiers of Dungeon Reward Chests , with each tier increasing in price and quality of loot.
The total Score achieved at the end of a Dungeon run dictates which Dungeon Reward Chests are unlocked. Completion of the floor unlocks the Wood , Gold , and Diamond chests; an A unlocks the Emerald chest; an S unlocks the Obsidian chest, and an S+ unlocks the Bedrock chest while on Floor V or higher. While on The Catacombs - Floor VII , you unlock an additional chest per phase of the boss fight completed.
- Floor I
- Floor II
- Floor III
- Floor IV
- Floor V
- Floor VI
- Floor VII

## Dungeonizing and Essence
Essence is a currency used in the Catacombs that can be spent on upgrades at various NPCs, used to upgrade items, and convert items to Dungeon items in a process colloquially known as ' dungeonizing '.
By converting an item to a Dungeon item, which can be seen through the tag at the bottom of an item's lore, it will grant increased stats while in the Catacombs. The stat boosts depend on your Catacombs level, the number of Star Upgrades the item has, and the number of Master Stars applied.
Standard Star Upgrades can be obtained on a variety of items that are not limited to being Catacombs-exclusive; however, Master Stars can only be applied to Dungeon items.

### Stat Bonuses
The stat bonuses from your Catacombs level and Star Upgrades are calculated separately and stack additively on top of the final state increase, only modifying the stats of the item itself.
While in the Catacombs, each Star Upgrade grants a +10% stat boost, adding up to a total stat boost of +50% ; each Master Star grants a +5% stat boost on top of the initial increase, totalling to a +75% increase in stats across the board.

### Item Quality
Dungeon items that drop from Dungeon Mobs and Minibosses will drop with different base stats depending on the floor it was dropped on and a randomly generated number that dictates the stat increase percentage.
There are up to 10 possible 'tiers' of base stats, dependent on the floor the item was dropped on.
  Tier
  Floor
  Standard
  Master Mode
  The Catacombs - Entrance The Catacombs - Floor I
  The Catacombs - Floor II
  The Catacombs - Floor III
  The Catacombs - Floor IV
  Master Mode - Floor I
  The Catacombs - Floor V
  Master Mode - Floor II
  The Catacombs - Floor VI
  Master Mode - Floor III
  The Catacombs - Floor VII
  Master Mode - Floor IV
  Master Mode - Floor V
  Master Mode - Floor VI
  10
  Master Mode - Floor VII
The bonus stats of dropped items can reach up to a +50% increase, which will result in its Rarity being upgraded.

## Dungeoneering
Dungeoneering is a Skill that is levelled up through completing runs of the Catacombs. As players complete or fail Dungeon runs, they will increment Catacombs XP and eventually upgrade their Catacombs skill. Each level grants increased ❤ Health and SkyBlock XP , and grants a multiplicative stat multiplier on Dungeon items of up to +475% .

## Trivia
- The Professor was referred to as Oak on the Alpha Hypixel Network . This was a reference to Professor Oak from the Pokémon franchise. The reason behind the change is unknown.
- This was a reference to Professor Oak from the Pokémon franchise. The reason behind the change is unknown.
- The Catacombs was intended to have 10 floors, with Maxor in Floor 7, Goldor in Floor 8, Storm in Floor 9, and Necron in Floor 10. The other Wither Lords were initially scrapped with the release of The Catacombs - Floor VII , but were re-added with the release of Master Mode - Floor VII .

  July 1, 2020
  0.7.11
  Dungeons infrastructure released onto the main server.
  The Catacombs, its 11 Floors and the Master Mode can be viewed in the Dungeon Hub.
  July 7, 2020
  0.8
  Released The Catacombs Dungeon.
  Released Catacombs Entrance and Floors I-III.
  July 14, 2020
  Added Boss Collections for all Catacombs bosses
  July 30, 2020
  Released Catacombs Floor IV.
  Added Ice Essence , which drops from Frozen Adventurers .
  Unstable Lost Adventurers now deal lightning damage; Holy ones heal faster.
  Added Frozen Adventurers to regular rooms, fixed an issue that was making them too tanky and gave them 1 extra Ice essence drop.
  Aug 1, 2020
  Mort won't give Dungeon Orbs anymore in Floor III and higher if the player does not have one already.
  Sep 17, 2020
  0.9.1
  Added stats to Golden and Diamond boss heads. On their respective floor, their stats are doubled.
  Dungeons stats are now added to the API.
  Floors II, III and IV are now approximately 5% easier
  Released Floor V.
  Starting Floor V, obtaining an S+ rank will unlock the Bedrock chest.
  Oct 1, 2020
  0.9.4
  Released Floor VI.
  Nov 17, 2020
  0.9.13
  Released Floor VII.
  The previously planned floors VIII, IX and X are now canceled.
  Floors I-VI are now slightly easier.
  Unknown Date
  Flight exploit with Spirit Boots in Floor VII boss room is patched.
  Jan 6, 2021
  Flight exploit with Tarantula Boots in Floor VII boss room fully patched.
  Mar 30, 2021
  0.11.3
  Added Master Mode, Floors I-V.
  Entrance now requires Combat level XV.
  Floor I now requires Catacombs I.
  Floor II now requires Catacombs III.
  Floor III now requires Catacombs V.
  Floor IV now requires Catacombs IX.
  Floor V now requires Catacombs XIV.
  Floor VI now requires Catacombs XIX.
  Floor VII now requires Catacombs XXIV.
  Reduced Catacombs level requirements for many items. Click here to see the full list of changes.
  Reduced Essence cost values for many items.
  From now on all current catacombs floor will grant more catacombs exp based on how many times you previously beaten that floor, up to 150% extra exp granted on floors 1 to 5, up to 100% on floor 6 and up to 50% extra on floor 7. This is not applied for Master Mode at this time.
  Apr 21, 2021
  0.11.4
  Added Master Mode, Floor VI.
  Aug 24, 2021
  Added 15 new rooms, found on every floor.
  Feb 24, 2022
  Master Mode Floor VII was leaked by 12 [ADMIN] Jayavarmen .
  Mar 1, 2022
  0.12.3
  Added Maxor , Storm , and Goldor to Floor VII.
  Made multiple changes to Floor VII.
  Mar 2, 2022
  Added Master Mode, Floor VII.

# The Catacombs - Floor I

- Regular
- Master Mode
The Catacombs - Floor I is the first floor in The Catacombs Dungeon with the 6 BOSS Bonzo .

## New Mobs
- 6 BOSS Bonzo
- Undead (Bonzo)

## New Items
- Bonzo's Staff (exclusive to Floor I)
- Bonzo's Mask (exclusive to Floor I)
- Necromancer's Brooch
- Red Nose (exclusive to Floor I)
- Enchanted Book (Rejuvenate, Bank, Ultimate Jerry, Combo, No Pain No Gain, Feather Falling)

## New Mechanics
- Players are automatically revived after 50 seconds.
- Up to 5 Dungeon Post-Boss Chests appear for looting when the 6 BOSS is defeated. These chests contain loot as well as Essence , and cost coins to open. Only 1 Chest may be opened per run, except if the player has a Dungeon Chest Key .
The Catacombs - Master Floor I is the first master floor in The Catacombs Dungeon with the 6 BOSS Master Bonzo .

## Boss
- 6 BOSS MASTER Bonzo ( 200M ❤ *2) Undead (Bonzo) ( 150M ❤ *Infinite)
- Undead (Bonzo) ( 150M ❤ *Infinite)

## New Items
- Master Skull (from Dungeon Reward Chest )

## New Mechanics
- Players are automatically revived after 50 seconds.
- Rare rewards now have a higher chance to appear in Dungeon Reward Chests .
- 5 Mini-Boss and 6 BOSS have high ❈ Defense starting from now.

## Dungeon Chest Loot
After each completed dungeon run in The Catacombs - Floor I and above the player is presented with Dungeon Reward Chests depending on how well they did. Listed here are the rewards from each chest:

### Music Discs
There is a 2% chance for the Essence in an Obsidian Dungeon Reward Chest to be replaced with one of these Music Discs :
- Dungeon Disc
- Clown Disc
- Necron Disc
- Watcher Disc
- Old Disc ( Master Mode )

  SkyBlock Prototype

  0.8
  Added The Catacombs - Floor I.
  Mar 30, 2021
  0.11.3
  Changed party size requirements from 4-5 to 2-5.
  Added The Catacombs Master Floor I.

# The Catacombs - Floor II

- Regular
- Master Mode
The Catacombs - Floor II is the second floor in the Catacombs Dungeon with 6 BOSS Scarf .

## New Mobs
- 6 BOSS Scarf
- Undead Archer
- Undead Mage
- Undead Priest
- Undead Warrior
- Watcher Undeads (Mr. Dead, Vader, Walker)
- Parasite
- Skeleton Master

## New Items
- Adaptive Blade (exclusive to Floor II)
- Scarf's Studies ( Thesis , Grimoire , exclusive to Floor II)
- Enchanted Book ( Ultimate Wise )
- Red Scarf (exclusive to Floor II)

## New Mechanics
- Players are automatically revived after 95 seconds.
- A new puzzle can appear: Higher or Lower (Blaze Puzzle).
The Catacombs - Floor II is the second master floor in the Catacombs Dungeon with 6 BOSS MASTER Scarf .

## Boss
- MASTER Scarf ( 375M ❤ ) Undead Archer ( 65M ❤ ) Undead Mage ( 60M ❤ ) Undead Priest ( 90M ❤ ) Undead Warrior ( 75M ❤ )
- Undead Archer ( 65M ❤ )
- Undead Mage ( 60M ❤ )
- Undead Priest ( 90M ❤ )
- Undead Warrior ( 75M ❤ )

## New Mechanics
- Players are automatically revived after 95 seconds.
- Scarf's Undeads (Undead Archer, Undead Mage, Undead Priest, Undead Warrior) spawns in a group of 2 for each type (8 in total).

## Dungeon Chest Loot
After each completed dungeon run in The Catacombs - Floor I and above the player is presented with Dungeon Reward Chest s depending on how well they did. Listed here are the rewards from each chest:

### Music Discs
There is a 2% chance for the Essence in an Obsidian Dungeon Reward Chest to be replaced with one of these Music Discs :
- Dungeon Disc
- Clown Disc
- Necron Disc
- Watcher Disc
- Old Disc ( Master Mode )

# The Catacombs - Floor III

- Regular
- Master Mode
The Catacombs - Floor III is the third floor of The Catacombs Dungeon with 6 BOSS The Professor .

## New Mobs
- 6 BOSS The Professor
- Guardians / Elder Guardians (Healthy, Reinforced, Laser, Chaos, Rogue)
- 5 Mini-Boss Shadow Assassin
- 5 Mini-Boss King Midas
- Watcher Undeads (Flamer, Skull, Bonzo )
- Skeletor
- Deathmite
- Zombie Soldier
- Zombie Knight
Zombie Grunt spawns are now replaced with Zombie Soldier and Knight spawns. Skeletor spawns replace Undead Skeleton spawns when 3 defeated Skeleton-type mobs merge. Scared Skeletons and Skeleton Grunts no longer spawn.

## New Items
- Adaptive Armor (exclusive to Floor III)
- Suspicious Vial (exclusive to Floor III)
- Enchanted Book ( Last Stand )
- Silent Death
- Midas Jewel
- Skeletor Armor
- Zombie Soldier Armor
- Zombie Knight Armor
- Zombie Soldier Cutlass
- Zombie Knight Sword

## New Mechanics
- Players will no longer automatically respawn.
- New puzzles can appear: Boulder, Ice Fill, and Ice Path.
- The Danger Room (Trap Room) appears from this floor on.
- Fairies in the Fairy room will only respawn up to 4 times.
Master Catacombs - Floor III is the third floor of Master Catacombs Dungeon with 6 BOSS MASTER The Professor .

## New Mobs
- 6 BOSS MASTER The Professor
- Guardians / Elder Guardians (Healthy, Reinforced, Laser, Chaos, Rogue)

## New Items
- First Master Star

## New Mechanics
- Players will no longer automatically respawn.
- New puzzles can appear: Boulder, Ice Fill, and Ice Path.
- The Danger Room (Trap Room) appears from this floor on.
- Fairies in the Fairy room will only respawn up to 4 times.

## Dungeon Chest Loot

### Music Discs
There is a 2% chance for the Essence in an Obsidian Dungeon Reward Chest to be replaced with one of these Music Discs :
- Dungeon Disc
- Clown Disc
- Necron Disc
- Watcher Disc
- Old Disc ( Master Mode )

  SkyBlock Prototype
  July 7, 2020
  0.8
  Added The Catacombs - Floor III.
  Sep 17, 2020
  0.9.1
  The Catacombs - Floor III become approximately 5% easier.

# The Catacombs - Floor IV

The Catacombs - Floor IV is the fourth floor of The Catacombs , featuring 6 BOSS Thorn as the boss of this floor.

## Overview
Floor IV introduces several new mobs and mechanics.
- You can no longer respawn naturally. The only way to respawn is with Revive Stones or if you have a Healer in your party. Fairies no longer respawn.
- The Watcher is assisted by two Watchful Eyes . They deal heavy damage to players who try to avoid Undead attacks by camping high places in the Blood Room.
- The Super Tank Zombie replaces Tank Zombie s, and two new mobs spawn: the Super Archer and Withermancer .
- The Frozen Adventurer has a chance to spawn as a mini-boss: their attacks compose of striking lightning to nearby players and using its Ice Spray Wand to stun you and amplify its damage dealt.
- The Treasure Talisman and Dungeon Chest Key have a chance to drop from Dungeon Secrets .
- The Quiz puzzle is available in this floor and all floors succeeding it.
- Scarf has a small chance to spawn as a Watcher Undead and drops a Scarf Fragment .
New obtainable items include:
- Spirit Sword
- Spirit Shortbow
- Spirit Boots
- Spirit Stone ( Spiritual )
- Spirit Wing ( Spirit Sceptre , Bone Necklace )
- Spirit Bone ( Bonemerang , Bone Reaver , Bone Necklace )
- Spirit Mask (exclusive to Master Mode)
- Spirit Pet
- Rend
- Ice Spray Wand
- Earth Shard
- Super Heavy Armor
- Bouncy Armor
- Treasure Talisman ( Treasure Ring , Treasure Artifact )
- Dungeon Chest Key

## Boss Fight
Upon entering Thorn 's arena, they will summon several Spirit Animals , each with unique abilities. Killing 25 Spirit Animals summons a Spirit Bear , which must be killed to drop a Spirit Bow . This Spirit Bow must then be fired at Thorn: 4 successful hits will kill Thorn, requiring 100 kills to defeat them.
While in Master Mode, 50 kills are required to summon a Spirit Bear, and Thorn dies in 6 hits instead, meaning 300 kills are required to defeat Thorn.

## Dungeon Chest Loot
Depending on the party's Dungeon Score in Floor IV , they will unlock higher tiers of Dungeon Reward Chests .
- The Wooden Chest , Gold Chest , and Diamond Chest are guaranteed;
- A is required to unlock the Emerald Chest ;
- S is required to unlock the Obsidian Chest .

### Music Discs
There is a 2% chance for the Essence in an Obsidian or Bedrock Dungeon Reward Chest to be replaced with one of these Music Discs :
- Dungeon Disc
- Clown Disc
- Necron Disc
- Watcher Disc
- Old Disc ( Master Mode )

## History
  SkyBlock Prototype
  July 30, 2020
  Added The Catacombs - Floor IV.
  Sep 17, 2020
  0.9.1
  The Catacombs - Floor IV become approximately 5% easier.
  Mar 30, 2021
  0.11.3
  Added Master Catacombs - Floor IV.

# The Catacombs - Floor V

The Catacombs - Floor V is the fifth floor of The Catacombs , featuring 6 BOSS Livid as the boss of this floor.

## Overview
Floor V introduces several new mobs and mechanics.
- The Bedrock Chest now spawns if the party achieves a score of S+ .
- Loot from Dungeon Reward Chests now have a small chance to have Stars applied to them.
- The Watcher will now apply modifiers to its Undead: these can be either Speedy , Stormy , Healthy , Boomer , Stealthy , or Golden .
- A Spirit Bear has a small chance to spawn as a Watcher Undead and drops a Thorn Fragment .
The only new mob that spawns here is the Fels .
New obtainable items include:
- Shadow Assassin Armor
- Livid Dagger
- Shadow Fury
- Last Breath
- Shadow Assassin Cloak
- Warped Stone
- Legion
- Overload
- Fel Pearl ( Fel Sword )

## Boss Fight
Upon commencing the boss fight, Livid will appear in the middle, surrounded by 8 Endermen: after a few seconds, the entire party is blinded temporarily and the Endermen turn into clones of Livid with different skins and colours. Among the clones hides the real Livid, which can be identified through the colouring of their name and the colouring of the terracotta on the ceiling.
Killing a clone will regenerate it to full health after a few seconds and fully heal the other clones. During Master Mode, the clones are capable of changing their skin and the colouring of the ceiling. These clones have the following abilities:
  Name
  Description
  Sword Attack
  Livid will throw a sword, dealing damage and teleporting to the target on hit.
  Ranged Attack
  Livid will strafe around any player who is sufficiently far away and shoot a bow, dealing damage on hit.
  Dash Attack
  Livid will dash at the player and deal damage to them.
  Wither Explosion
  Livid will shoot a Wither Skull that explodes on impact.
  Damage Potion
  Livid will throw damage potions, dealing ✷ True Damage .
  Blindness Potion
  Livid will throw potions of blindness, leaving an AoE effect that causes blindness.
  Teleport Attack
  Livid will teleport away from the player if they are close enough.
Identifying the correct Livid clone and killing it will end the boss fight and defeat him.

## Dungeon Chest Loot
Depending on the party's Dungeon Score in Floor V , they will unlock higher tiers of Dungeon Reward Chests .
- The Wooden Chest , Gold Chest , and Diamond Chest are guaranteed;
- A is required to unlock the Emerald Chest ;
- S is required to unlock the Obsidian Chest ;
- S+ is required to unlock the Bedrock Chest .
- Regular

### Music Discs
There is a 2% chance for the Essence in an Obsidian or Bedrock Dungeon Reward Chest to be replaced with one of these Music Discs :
- Dungeon Disc
- Clown Disc
- Necron Disc
- Watcher Disc
- Old Disc ( Master Mode )

# The Catacombs - Floor VI

The Catacombs - Floor VI is the sixth floor of The Catacombs , featuring 6 BOSS Sadan as the boss of this floor.

## Overview
Floor VI introduces several new mobs and mechanics.
- A Mimic has a chance to spawn when claiming a Secret , and can be killed to obtain the Mimic Fragment , used to craft the Lesser Orb of Healing : unlike regular secrets, killing a Mimic grants +2 Dungeon Score .
- A Skeletor Prime has a 50% chance to spawn in place of a Skeletor .
- Livid has a small chance to spawn as a Watcher Undead and drops a Livid Fragment .
- Loot from Dungeon Reward Chests now have a small chance to have a Recombobulator 3000 applied to them.
New mobs that appear include:
- Skeletor Prime
- Mimic
- Zombie Commander
New obtainable items include:
- Giant's Sword
- Ancient Rose ( Fel Rose )
- Flower of Truth ( Bouquet of Lies )
- Fel Skull ( Felthorn Reaper )
- Necromancer Lord Armor
- Necromancer Sword
- Soulweaver Gloves
- Summoning Ring
- Sadan's Brooch
- Swarm
- Livid Fragment
- Mimic Fragment
- Zombie Commander Armor
- Zombie Commander Whip

## Boss Fight
Sadan 's boss fight consists of 3 phases.
6 Sleeping Golem s surround the arena: upon being attacked, they will transform into Woke Golem s and attack the player, dealing immense damage and moving at substantial speed. They drop Ancient Roses , which can be crafted into the Flower of Truth and Fel Rose , the latter of which are used to craft the Bouquet of Lies and Felthorn Reaper .

### Phase 1: Terracotta
During the first phase, 20 Terracotta s stand alongside a long red carpet. Once Sadan 's dialogue concludes, the Terracotta s will begin attacking the players using flower projectiles; if the player is above the Terracotta attacking them, they will take more damage.
After being killed, the Terracotta s will turn into skulls on the ground for 10s before reviving at full health.
During this period, a timer labelled Sadan's Interest Meter ticks down every second for 120s : killing a Terracotta reduces this timer by 1s . Once Sadan's Interest Meter is fully depleted, the phase concludes.

### Phase 2: Giants
During the second phase, Sadan will summon 4 giants: The Diamond Giant , L.A.S.R. , Bigfoot , and the Jolly Pink Giant . All four of them have different abilities.
During Master Mode , 4 Mutant Giants that have the combined abilities of all four aforementioned giants will spawn in place of the regular four.
  Image
  Name
  Ability
  The Diamond Giant
  Sword of 10,000 Truths: The Diamond Giant will attack players with the Sword of 10,000 Truths, dealing heavy damage. This ability mimics the Giant's Sword .
  L.A.S.R.
  L.A.S.R. Eye Beam: L.A.S.R. will shoot out a laser beam from their eyes that never misses: it deals increased damage over time.
  Bigfoot
  Stomp: Bigfoot will jump into the sky and land on the ground, dealing heavy damage and knockback.
  Jolly Pink Giant
  Boulder Toss: The Jolly Pink Giant will throw a chunk of terrain at nearby players, dealing heavy damage. This ability mimics the Yeti Sword .
Once all four giants are dead, the phase will conclude.

### Phase 3: Sadan
During the third and final phase, Sadan will lower a chain into the ground, revealing a stronger giant: The Giant One . After a brief section of dialogue, Sadan will enter The Giant One and fuse with him, commencing the final phase.
The Giant One combines all four abilities of the previous four giants, and deals significantly more damage than them. In Master Mode, all four Mutant Giants are also respawned: once The Giant One is killed, the fight concludes regardless of all other circumstances.

## Dungeon Chest Loot
Depending on the party's Dungeon Score in Floor VI , they will unlock higher tiers of Dungeon Reward Chests .
- The Wooden Chest , Gold Chest , and Diamond Chest are guaranteed;
- A is required to unlock the Emerald Chest ;
- S is required to unlock the Obsidian Chest ;
- S+ is required to unlock the Bedrock Chest .

### Music Discs
There is a 2% chance for the Essence in an Obsidian or Bedrock Dungeon Reward Chest to be replaced with one of these Music Discs :
- Dungeon Disc
- Clown Disc
- Necron Disc
- Watcher Disc
- Old Disc ( Master Mode )

# The Catacombs - Floor VII

The Catacombs - Floor VII is the seventh and final floor of The Catacombs , featuring 7 FINAL-BOSS Maxor , Storm , Goldor , and Necron as the bosses. The Wither King appears in a 5th phase during Master Mode .

## Overview
Floor VII introduces several new mechanics.
- Several mobs are exclusive to Floor VII : the Zombie Lord , Skeleton Lord , Wither Miner , Wither Guard , and Necron's Apostle .
- A Skeletor Prime has a 100% chance to spawn in place of a Skeletor .
- The Ice Fill puzzle is exclusive to this floor.
New mobs that appear include:
- Zombie Lord
- Skeleton Lord
New obtainable items include:
- Wither Armor
- Necron's Handle
- Wither Catalyst
- Precursor Gear
- Wither Blood
- Wither Cloak Sword
- Auto Recombobulator
- Diamante's Handle
- L.A.S.R.'s Eye
- Jolly Pink Rock
- Bigfoot's Bola
- Soul Eater
- One For All
- Zombie Lord Armor
- Skeleton Lord Armor
- Implosion , Wither Shield , and Shadow Warp
- Dark Claymore (M7 exclusive)
New craftable items include:
- Necron's Blade
- Hyperion
- Valkyrie
- Astraea
- Scylla
- Necron's Armor
- Storm's Armor
- Goldor's Armor
- Maxor's Armor
- Catacombs Expert Ring
- Wither Relic

## Boss Fight
NOTE: Most teleportation abilities are disabled during the fight, including:
- Aspect of the End
- Aspect of the Void
- Etherwarp Conduit
- Sinseeker Scythe
- Ender Pearls
- Grappling Hook
- Leaping Sword
- Silk-Edge Sword

### Phase 1: Maxor
Maxor's arena: players must collect Energy Crystals and lure Maxor to a beam to damage him.
Maxor 's phase takes place in a factory. Players must collect Energy Crystals , located at the top of the arena, by completing a series of parkour and place them at platforms located near the bottom of the arena. Once this is completed, Maxor must be lured to the end of the arena to be damaged by a beam. Once Maxor dies, the party progresses to the next phase.
Maxor has the following attacks:
  Name
  Description
  Wither Skulls
  Maxor will rapidly shoot 3 Wither Skulls at the target, dealing large ❁ Damage and ⬱ Knockback .
  Rapid Fire Skulls
  Maxor will stop moving and begin rapidly firing Wither Skulls, dealing large ❁ Damage and ⬱ Knockback .
  Detonate
  Maxor will spawn and detonate a block of TNT, exploding after several seconds, dealing large ❁ Damage and ⬱ Knockback .
  Maxor's Rage
  Upon being damaged by the beam, Maxor will become enraged and begin summoning frequent explosions around him.
A Bonzo's Staff or Jerry-chine Gun can be used for mobility during this phase.

### Phase 2: Storm
Storm's arena: players must lure Storm under a pillar and crush him using the corresponding pressure pads.
Storm 's phase takes place in a large arena with a main platform in the middle and four platforms in the corners, connected by thin bridges. Four pillars are found in the main platform, which are connected to four corresponding pressure pads in the corners: players must lure Storm underneath a pillar while another player activates its corresponding pressure pad, crushing Storm in the process.
If the party fails to kill Storm and no functioning pillars are left, the run will be softlocked and players will have to respawn.
Storm has the following attacks:
  Name
  Description
  Wither Skulls
  Storm will rapidly shoot 3 Wither Skulls at the target, dealing large ❁ Damage and ⬱ Knockback .
  Lightning Fireball
  Storm will shoot fireballs at nearby players, dealing large ❁ Damage and ⬱ Knockback .
  Static Field
  Storm will summon lots of lightning around the arena, dealing large ❁ Damage to all players who are hit.
  Giga Lightning
  Storm will fly to the center of the arena and stop moving, charging up a Giga Lightning for 10s , before summoning lightning throughout the entire arena, instantly killing everyone who is not standing under a functional pillar: this can be bypassed with a Wither Cloak Sword , Mithril Coat , or Gyrokinetic Wand . During Master Mode, the charge time is reduced to 5s .
  Storm's Rage
  Upon being crushed by the pillar, Storm will become enraged and begin summoning frequent explosions around him.

### Phase 3: Goldor
See also: Terminals
Goldor's arena: players must complete terminals and devices and flick levers to open the gate.
Goldor 's phase takes place in a factory composed of corridors in the outline of a square, concluding with a path extending into the Core Entrance. Players must both complete a series of parkour, solving Terminals at the same time, while slowing down Goldor as he slowly approaches.
The Core Entrance, where Goldor can be damaged.
Once all Terminals are completed and all levers and activated, the gate will be destroyed and the party can progress: the final section leads into the Core Entrance, where Goldor will close in on the party. During this period, Goldor can be damaged: successfully killing Goldor in time will allow the party to progress to the fourth phase.
Goldor has the following attacks:
  Name
  Description
  Greatsword
  Goldor will fly in a player's direction, dealing immense ❁ Damage and ⬱ Knockback on impact.
  Detonate
  Goldor will detonate sets of TNT located near the ceiling, igniting them and dealing immense ❁ Damage and ⬱ Knockback to nearby players.
  Instakill
  All players who are behind Goldor's path of movement will be instantly killed.

### Phase 4: Necron
Necron's arena: players must damage him continually while avoiding his attacks.
Necron 's phase takes place in a circular arena with a platform in the middle, surrounded by a lava moat. Necron will use his abilities against the players: after taking enough damage, he gives the players blindness and teleports to the middle platform.
Unlike the other bosses, Necron will always be able to be damaged traditionally. Once Necron is defeated, the run is completed and players can claim loot: during Master Mode, killing Necron will allow players to progress to the fifth phase.
Necron has the following abilities:
  Name
  Description
  Wither Skulls
  Necron will rapidly shoot 3 Wither Skulls at the target, dealing more ❁ Damage and ⬱ Knockback than Maxor or Storm .
  Empowered Greatsword
  Necron will summon 4 greatswords, similar to Goldor , rotating around Necron and flying towards a random level, dealing immense ❁ Damage on impact.
  Lightning Fireball
  Necron will shoot fireballs at nearby players, dealing large ❁ Damage and ⬱ Knockback .
  Static Field
  Necron will summon lots of lightning around the arena, dealing large ❁ Damage to all players who are hit.
  Laser Wall
  Necron will cast 64 Laser beams that rotate clockwise. Contact with those laser beams deal 25% of their ❤ Health as ✷ True Damage , akin to Broken Heart Radiation used by the Tier IV Voidgloom Seraph .
  Nuclear Frenzy
  Necron will move towards the center platform and begins exploding rapidly every second: taking damage reduces the size of the explosion, and not taking damage will increase it. After a certain threshold, the Nuclear Frenzy will end.
  Necron's Rage
  Necron will stay still and fire a dozen Wither Skulls at a nearby player, dealing large ❁ Damage and ⬱ Knockback .

### Phase 5: Kaeman
Kaeman's arena: players must kill each Withered Dragon near its corresponding statue.
The Wither King 's phase, exclusive to Master Mode - Floor VII , takes place in a giant arena surrounded by giant statues of dragons. Players must collect Corrupted Relics around the arena and place them, summoning the Wither King and two Withered Dragons . Apostle s will also spawn.
There are 5 Withered Dragons , each of which must be killed while near their corresponding statue to be successfully completed. A list of Withered Dragons are found below:
  Name
  Behaviour
  Apex Dragon
  Apex will swoop down and attack nearby players, dealing immense ❁ Damage and knockback on impact.
  Soul Dragon
  Soul will teleport to random locations throughout the arena, and will teleport to a random statue (including its own) every 3 times it teleports.
  Flame Dragon
  Flame will shoot players with fireballs and occasionally swoop down, leaving behind a trail of fire as it flies.
  Ice Dragon
  Ice will occasionally swoop down, leaving behind a trail of ice that heavily restricts movement and trapping players in cubes of ice.
  Power Dragon
  Power will occasionally fly towards the center of the arena and perform a Mega TNT attack, which can be prevented if enough damage is dealt: a successful Mega TNT will deal immense ✷ True Damage to anyone in the center of the arena.
The Wither King also has some attacks of his own:
  Name
  Behaviour
  Reel In
  The Wither King will pull players who get too close to it using its tentacles and instantly kill them.
  Atomizing Ray
  The Wither King will shoot a giant beam from its head and look throughout the arena, dealing colossal damage to players standing within.
  Dimensional Slash
  The Wither King will randomly strike players with lightning.
Once all dragons are alive at the same time, a hand reaches up from the center of the arena, grabbing all players in the party and killing them instantly, resulting in a fail. Once all dragons are dead, the run will be completed.

## Loot
The Catacombs - Floor VII 's Dungeon Reward Chests function slightly differently: players will unlock higher-tiered chests as they progress. Reaching the boss fight unlocks the Wood chest, beating Maxor unlocks the Gold chest, beating Storm unlocks the Diamond chest, beating Goldor unlocks the Emerald Chest, beating Necron unlocks the Obsidian chest, and beating The Wither King automatically unlocks the Bedrock chest.
Wither Armor pieces and Necron's Handles obtained from Master Mode - Floor VII have a small chance to get a cosmetic Shiny prefix. The item will also have an enchantment glint even if it is not enchanted.
- Regular
- Master Mode
  Chest
  Drop
  Chance
  Cost
  Default

### Music Discs
There is a 2% chance for the Essence in an Obsidian or Bedrock Dungeon Reward Chest to be replaced with one of these Music Discs :
- Dungeon Disc
- Clown Disc
- Necron Disc
- Watcher Disc
- Old Disc ( Master Mode )

## Trivia
- When the floor first released, Goldor's phase was bugged and could not be completed.
- When Master Mode - Floor VII released, Shiny Wither Armor had the same scaling mechanic as most Dungeon Mob drops, adding up to a +50% stat boost and upgrading its base rarity in the case of a perfect stat boost.

## History
  SkyBlock Prototype
  July 1, 2020
  0.7.11
  The Catacombs - Floor VII can be viewed in Mort .
  The boss of Floor VII was originally Maxor, the Young Wither.
  Nov 17, 2020
  0.9.13
  The boss of Floor VII was changed to Necron .
  Released The Catacombs - Floor VII .
  Nov 17, 2020
  0.9.13
  Fixed bugged 3rd phase.
  Fixed being able to use ender pearls in the boss room.
  Dec 7, 2020
  Fixed exploit with Spirit Boots which allowed flight within the boss room.
  Jan 6, 2021
  Fixed exploit with Tarantula Boots which allowed flight within the boss room.
  Mar 30, 2021
  0.11.3
  Fixed exploit with Rabbit Hat which granted jump boost within the boss room.
  June 26, 2021
  Fixed the Etherwarp Conduit ability working in the boss room.
  Aug 27, 2021
  Fixed exploit where the Energy Crystals in the 1st phase could be taken out of the Dungeon.
  Mar 1, 2022
  0.12.3
  Added Maxor , Storm , and Goldor to The Catacombs - Floor VII .
  Increased Catacombs XP and loot from The Catacombs - Floor VII .
  Mar 2, 2022
  Added The Master Mode Catacombs - Floor VII .
  Added Dark Claymore drop from Dungeon Reward Chests in Master Mode.
  Added Master Skull - Tier 5 drop from Dungeon Reward Chests in Master Mode.
  Added Fifth Master Star drop from Dungeon Reward Chests in Master Mode.
  Added Thunderlord VII drop from Dungeon Reward Chests in Master Mode.
  May 31, 2023
  0.18.5
  Increased chest price for Necron's Handle from 35 million to 100 million
  Increased chest price for Implosion from 3.3 million to 50 million
  Increased chest price for Wither Shield from 3.3 million to 50 million
  Increased chest price for Shadow Warp from 3.3 million to 50 million

# Dungeon Hub

The Dungeon Hub is accessible through the Hub Island via a portal at -45, 88, 13 (through a staircase in the Southwest area) or by using the Fast Travel feature in the SkyBlock Menu. This area has been made as a means to access all existing Dungeons and all Dungeon-related shops in one place.
Damage (noticeably, Fall Damage ) is disabled in the Dungeon Hub.
NOTE: The Fast Travel warp is not unlocked if the player has not gone through the Portal.

## Tasks
This text is shown when a player enters ⏣ Dungeon Hub for the first time:

## Tasks
When the player first enters ⏣ Dungeon Hub , they will be greeted with the following message:
These are the additional tasks:
- Play with Friends!
- Create your own custom party.
- Find Fairy Souls (7)
- Hub Racing (for Wither Essence and Speed Accessories. Located under the main dungeon area)

## Purpose
The main purpose of the Dungeon Hub is to queue into the Catacombs and Kuudra . Mort allows the player to queue into Dungeons through Party Finder; Malik allows the player to upgrade items with Essence , dungeonise gear, apply Reforges , and salvage items; and Ophelia serves as a shop for lots of convenient Dungeon items and powerful gear, like the Wither Goggles , Giant Cleaver , Death Bow , Steel Chestplate , and Mender Crown .
Crag allows the player to access Kuudra , and Vulcan provides a shop for Crimson Essence . Vesuvius can also be found in the ⏣ Forgotten Skull , who serves a similar purpose to Croseus.
Croesus also allows the player to open unclaimed Dungeon Reward Chests and Kuudra Chests for 72 hours, and completing The Catacombs - Floor III allows the player to access the Catacombs without a party by giving Saul's Recommendation to Mort.

## Hub Racing
Players can do the Hub Racing quest by talking with Guildford and selecting which destination and type of race.
There are 3 different race routes:
- Crystal Core
- Giant Mushroom
- Precursor Ruins
Each route has 4 types of race:
- Anything (can use Abilities (like Aspect of the End / Aspect of the Void , Leaping Sword / Silk-Edge Sword ), Ender Pearls , and Grappling Hook )
- No Pearls (can use Abilities as stated above, but no Ender Pearls}}
- No Abilities (can use only the Grappling Hook)
- Nothing at all (can't use anything, and walking speed is capped at 130)
The player can choose whether or not they want to race with runback, where they must reach the goal and then run back to the start. With no runback they will be teleported back to Guildford after reaching the goal. 
In total, there are 24 different Dungeon Hub races.
For every race the player completes in time, Guildford will give 3/4/5/6 Wither Essence or a Cat Talisman Upgrade.
Players can obtain the Speed Accessories by completing (4/4) objectives in at least 1 category in a location. For the rewards, the order of the races doesn't matter.
For example, completing 4/4 objectives on Precursor Ruins + Anything + Runback would reward a Cat Talisman , then completing 4/4 objectives on Precursor Ruins + Nothing at all + No Runback afterwards would reward a Lynx Talisman .
Each reward upgrades the previous:
- Cat Talisman - +1 ✦ Speed UNCOMMON Accessory
- Lynx Talisman - +2 ✦ Speed RARE Accessory
- Cheetah Talisman - +3 ✦ Speed EPIC Accessory
